class=\"content-area col-sm-12 col-md-6\"><main id=\"content\" class=\"site-content\" role=\"main\"><article id=\"post-5715\" class=\"post-5715 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-wordpress tag-administrator tag-author tag-editor tag-logged-in tag-logged_in tag-subscriber tag-the_content tag-wordpress main-hentry\"><header class=\"entry-header\"><strong class=\"text-uppercase margin-bottom-15 display-block category-meta\"><a class=\"wordpress\" href=\"https://martech.zone/content/wordpress/\" title=\"View all posts in WordPress\">WordPress</a></strong><h1 class=\"entry-title  margin-bottom-30\">Restrict Pages in WordPress to Require a Login</h1><div class=\"entry-meta margin-bottom-30 hidden-print\" style=\"\">\n\t<div class=\"sparkle-sharrre-counter sharrre-counter shares-counter display-inline-block text-center\">\n\t<strong class=\"shares-count display-block primary-color\" data-service=\"facebook\" data-url=\"https://martech.zone/login-content-wordpress-page-template/\">0</strong> <small class=\"share-text display-block\" data-singular=\"Share\">Shares</small>\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"sparkle-sharrre-with-entry-meta display-inline-block\">\n\t<div class=\"social-share-buttons sparkle-sharrre-buttons style-color size-large\" data-url=\"https://martech.zone/login-content-wordpress-page-template/\" data-title=\"Restrict Pages in WordPress to Require a Login\" data-source=\"https://martech.zone/\" data-media=\"https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Screen-Shot-2013-07-01-at-12.23.52-PM.png\"><span title=\"Share on Facebook\" class=\"facebook\" data-service=\"facebook\" data-service=\"more\" data-show=\"true\"><i class=\"fa fa-ellipsis-h\"></i><label class=\"hidden-xs hidden\">More services</label></span></div>\n\t<div class=\"gray-icon clearfix\"><span class=\"post-meta-info byline\"><span class=\"author vcard\"><a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://martech.zone/author/douglaskarr/\"><img src=\"https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/022a8c9292b6e9e20f3b9b34cf2dddd3?s=32&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g\" width=\"32\" height=\"32\" alt=\"\" class=\"avatar avatar-32 wp-user-avatar wp-user-avatar-32 photo avatar-default\"> Douglas Karr</a></span></span><span class=\"post-meta-info posted-on\"><i class=\"fa fa-clock-o\"></i> <time class=\"entry-date published\" datetime=\"2009-09-28T23:39:19+00:00\">Monday, September 28, 2009</time><time class=\"updated hidden\" datetime=\"2013-10-11T02:27:42+00:00\">Friday, October 11, 2013</time></span></div></div>\n\t</div><div class=\"entry-thumbnail margin-bottom-30\"><div class=\"post-thumbnail\"><div class=\"thumb-w\"><img width=\"263\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Screen-Shot-2013-07-01-at-12.23.52-PM-263x400.png\" class=\"attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Screen-Shot-2013-07-01-at-12.23.52-PM-263x400.png 263w, https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Screen-Shot-2013-07-01-at-12.23.52-PM-131x200.png 131w, https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Screen-Shot-2013-07-01-at-12.23.52-PM-66x100.png 66w, https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Screen-Shot-2013-07-01-at-12.23.52-PM-197x300.png 197w, https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Screen-Shot-2013-07-01-at-12.23.52-PM-171x260.png 171w, https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Screen-Shot-2013-07-01-at-12.23.52-PM-59x90.png 59w, https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Screen-Shot-2013-07-01-at-12.23.52-PM.png 282w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 263px) 100vw, 263px\"></div></div></div></header><div class=\"entry-content\"><p><img src=\"https://c.martech.zone/wp-content/uploads/2009/09/login_lock.jpg\" class=\"s3-img alignright\" border=\"0\" alt=\"login_lock.jpg\" align=\"right\">This week, we were finishing up implementing a custom theme on a client site and they requested that we build some kind of interaction where some of the pages were restricted to registered subscribers. At first, we thought about implementing third party plugins, but the solution was actually quite simple.</p><div class=\"entry-stuff margin-bottom-15 hidden-print single-post-ads-top pull-right-sm pull-right-md pull-right-lg margin-left-15 text-center-xs\"><div id=\"bsap_877\" class=\"bsap\" data-serve=\"C6YD4KT\"></div></div><p>First, we copied the page template to a new file (any name is fine, just maintain the php extension). At the top of the page, be sure to comment on the page so that you can see it in the template editor by name:<br> <code>&lt;?php /* Template Name: Subscribers Only */ ?&gt;</code></p><p>Next, look for the line in your page’s code that displays the content. It should look like this:<br> <code>&lt;?php the_content(); ?&gt;</code></p><p>Now, you’ll need to wrap some code around that line:<br> <code>&lt;?php global $user_ID; get_currentuserinfo(); ?&gt;<br> &lt;?php if($user_ID) { ?&gt;<br> &lt;h2&gt;&lt;?php the_title(); ?&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;<br> &lt;?php the_content(); ?&gt;<br> &lt;?php } else { ?&gt;<br> &lt;h2&gt;Subscriber Only&lt;/h2&gt;<br> &lt;p&gt;We're sorry, the content you are trying to reach is restricted to subscribers only.&lt;/p&gt;<br> &lt;?php } ?&gt;</code></p><p>The code starts by checking the session to see if the user is logged into your <a title=\"WordPress\" href=\" https://martech.zone/wordpress/\">WordPress</a> site. If they are logged in, the content is displayed. If they are not logged in, the message states that you are trying to reach restricted content.</p><p>In order to utilize the page, you’ll need to select the <strong>Subscribers Only</strong> page template in the advanced section of your page’s options (on the sidebar). That will restrict the page to readers who are logged in.</p><p>If you’d like to get really fancy, you can add a login and logout method to your sidebar as well:<br> <code>&lt;?php global $user_ID; get_currentuserinfo(); ?&gt;<br> &lt;?php if($user_ID) { ?&gt;<br> &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=\"&lt;?php echo wp_logout_url(); ?&gt;\"&gt;Logout&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br> &lt;?php } else { ?&gt;<br> &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=\"&lt;?php get_settings('home'); ?&gt;/wp-login.php\"&gt;Customer Login&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br> &lt;?php } ?&gt;</code></p> <span class=\"cp-load-after-post\"></span><p></p><div class=\"entry-stuff clear margin-bottom-15 hidden-print single-post-ads-bottom text-center\"><div id=\"bsap_2384\" class=\"bsap\" data-serve=\"CVAIV2QM\"></div></div></div><footer class=\"entry-meta
